        function GetBubbleChartFormatData(dataplot, CustomColors) {
            var BubbleData = [];
            var AveragePos = 1;
            var RiskPos = 2;
            var FundSizePos = 3;
            for (var i = 0; i < dataplot.LstRatioDataReturn.length; i++) {
                var Series = {};
                var valArr = [];
                var SeriesData = [[]];
                var LstKeyvaluePair = dataplot.LstRatioDataReturn[i].LstKeyValuePair;
                ////
                valArr.push(parseFloat(LstKeyvaluePair[AveragePos].Value), parseFloat(LstKeyvaluePair[RiskPos].Value), 1);
                //valArr.push(parseFloat(LstKeyvaluePair[AveragePos].Value), parseFloat(LstKeyvaluePair[RiskPos].Value), parseFloat(LstKeyvaluePair[FundSizePos].Value));
                SeriesData.push(valArr);
                SeriesData.shift();
                Series.name = LstKeyvaluePair[0].Value;
                Series.data = SeriesData;
                if (dataplot.LstRatioDataReturn[i].SchemeId == dataplot.SchemeId) {
                    // //
                    Series.color = '#000000';
                    Series.marker = {
                        fillOpacity: 1
                    };
                }
                else {
                    Series.color = CustomColors[i];
                    Series.marker = {
                        fillOpacity: 1
                    };
                }
                BubbleData.push(Series);
            }
            return BubbleData;
        };

            var tt = [[]];
            var tt1 = {};
            tt1.name = "Aggregated Portfolio";

            var points = [];
            if (dataPortReturn != null) {
                for (var j = 0; j < dataPortReturn.length; j += 1) {
                    var res = dataPortReturn[j].Date.split("-");
                    points.push([Date.UTC(res[0], res[1] - 1, res[2]), dataPortReturn[j].OrginalValue, dataPortReturn[j].StrValue]);
                }
            }
            tt1.data = points;
            tt.push(tt1);

            tt.shift();
            GenerateGraph('nav', 'DvReturnAnalysis', tt, '', '', 'In %', '', '', '', '', '', true, true, yxchartstyle, titlechartstyle, subtitlechartstyle, legendstyle, navspecialprop, CustomColors, decPlace);





















            setTimeout(function () {
                //////----------------SGV download
                var chart3 = $('#DvReturnAnalysis').highcharts();


                var chartReturnAnalysis = chart3.getSVG({
                    scrollbar: { enabled: false },
                    navigator: { enabled: false },
                    
                });

                //var svgData = chartInstrumentAllocation.getSVG();
                var svgBlob = new Blob([chartReturnAnalysis], { type: "image/svg+xml;charset=utf-8" });
                var svgUrl = URL.createObjectURL(svgBlob);
                var downloadLink = document.createElement("a");
                downloadLink.href = svgUrl;
                downloadLink.download = "ImgReturnAnalysis.svg";
                document.body.appendChild(downloadLink);
                downloadLink.click();
                document.body.removeChild(downloadLink);
                /////end svg
            }, 1000);
        }

        function GetTreemapFormatData(dataplot, clrlst) {
            if (dataplot != null) {
                // var data = dataConsolidated.LstNavReturnModel;
                var tt = [];
                var j = 0;
                for (var i = 0; i < dataplot.length; i += 1) {
                    var tt1 = {};
                    tt1.id = dataplot[i].AmcId;
                    tt1.name = dataplot[i].AmcName + " (" + dataplot[i].StrAumPercent + "%)";
                    tt1.value = parseFloat(dataplot[i].StrAumPercent);
                    tt1.NameToDisplay = dataplot[i].AmcName + " (" + dataplot[i].StrAumPercent + "%)";

                    tt1.color = clrlst[j];
                    j = j + 1;
                    if (clrlst.length == j) { j = 0; }

                    tt.push(tt1);
                }

                return tt;
            }
            else {
                return null;
            }

        }
